    WHERE [u].[id] IN (2346, 2343, 2342, 2339, 2339, 2336, 2333, 2331, 2338, 2419, 2337, 2413, 2416, 2349) AND ((CONVERT(date, [c].[history_date]) >= @__dst_1) AND (CONVERT(date, [c].[history_date]) <= @__ded_2))
    ORDER BY [c].[id] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_3 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_4 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [collection_add_contact] AS [c0] ON [t].[add_id] = [c0].[id]

LEFT JOIN [users] AS [u0] ON [c1].[call_by] = [u0].[id]
ORDER BY [t].[id] DESC
